[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m ﻿=== 1.3.7 / 2010-05-13
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m 
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m NOTE:
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m 
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m http://rubygems.org is now the default source for downloading gems.
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m 
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m You may have sources set via ~/.gemrc, so you should replace
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m http://gems.rubyforge.org with http://rubygems.org
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m 
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m http://gems.rubyforge.org will continue to work for the forseeable future.
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m 
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m New features:
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m 
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m * `gem` commands
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m   * `gem install` and `gem fetch` now report alternate platforms when a
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m     matching one couldn't be found.
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m   * `gem contents` --prefix is now the default as specified in --help.  Bug
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m     #27211 by Mamoru Tasaka.
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m   * `gem fetch` can fetch of old versions again.  Bug #27960 by Eric Hankins.
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m   * `gem query` and friends output now lists platforms.  Bug #27856 by Greg
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m     Hazel.
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m   * `gem server` now allows specification of multiple gem dirs for
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m     documentation.  Bug #27573 by Yuki Sonoda.
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m   * `gem unpack` can unpack gems again.  Bug #27872 by Timothy Jones.
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m   * `gem unpack` now unpacks remote gems.
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m   * --user-install is no longer the default.  If you really liked it, see
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m     Gem::ConfigFile to learn how to set it by default.  (This change was made
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m     in 1.3.6)
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m * RubyGems now has platform support for IronRuby.  Patch #27951 by Will Green.
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m 
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m Bug fixes:
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m 
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m * Require rubygems/custom_require if --disable-gem was set.  Bug #27700 by
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m   Roger Pack.
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m * RubyGems now protects against exceptions being raised by plugins.
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m * rubygems/builder now requires user_interaction.  Ruby Bug #1040 by Phillip
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m   Toland.
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m * Gem::Dependency support #version_requirements= with a warning.  Fix for old
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m   Rails versions.  Bug #27868 by Wei Jen Lu.
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m * Gem::PackageTask depends on the package dir like the other rake package
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m   tasks so dependencies can be hooked up correctly.
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m 
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m 
[36mec2-75-101-215-56.compute-1.amazonaws.com[0m ------------------------------------------------------------------------------
